Use this vocabulary when the issue concerns **hierarchy**, **presence**, **absence**, **trace**, **supplement**, **writing**, **undecidability**, or **internal instability**.  
  
Core vocabulary: **Deconstruction (解构; fr: déconstruction)**, **Metaphysics of Presence (在场形而上学; fr: métaphysique de la présence)**, **Trace (痕迹; fr: trace)**, **Supplement (补充; fr: supplément)**, **Différance (延异; fr: différance)**, **Writing (书写; fr: écriture)**, **Pharmakon (药/毒; el: φάρμακον)**, **Undecidability (不可判定性; fr: indécidabilité)**, **Aporia (难题; el: ἀπορία; fr: aporie)**.  
  
**Problem solved:** this vocabulary reveals how a system depends on what it subordinates or excludes.  
(这一词汇揭示一个系统如何依赖其所贬低或排除之物。)  
  
**Use when asking:**  
What hierarchy is being stabilized? What secondary term is secretly necessary? What trace remains inside the privileged term?  
(什么等级正在被稳定？什么次要项其实是必要的？什么痕迹留在被优先项内部？)  
  
**Typical sentence:** The text privileges speech over writing, but its account of speech already depends on repeatability, absence, and trace.  
(文本把言语优先于书写，但其言语理论已经依赖重复性、缺席和痕迹。)  
  
**Misuse warning:** deconstruction is not reversal. It does not simply make the excluded term superior. It shows that the hierarchy cannot secure itself.  
(解构不是反转。它并不只是让被排除项变得更优越，而是显示等级无法自我保证。)  
  
### 7. If the Problem Is “What Produced This Truth?”, Use Foucauldian Vocabulary  
  
Use this vocabulary when the issue concerns **discourse**, **archive**, **power/knowledge**, **normalization**, **discipline**, **biopolitics**, **governmentality**, or **subjectivation**.  
  
Core vocabulary: **Discourse (话语; fr: discours)**, **Archive (档案; fr: archive)**, **Statement (陈述; fr: énoncé)**, **Episteme (认识型; el: ἐπιστήμη; fr: épistémè)**, **Power/Knowledge (权力/知识; fr: savoir-pouvoir; en: power/knowledge)**, **Regime of Truth (真理体制; fr: régime de vérité)**, **Discipline (规训; fr: discipline)**, **Normalization (规范化; fr: normalisation)**, **Biopolitics (生命政治; fr: biopolitique)**, **Governmentality (治理术; fr: gouvernementalité)**.  
  
**Problem solved:** this vocabulary reveals how truths, subjects, bodies, and norms are historically produced through institutions and practices.  
(这一词汇揭示真理、主体、身体和规范如何通过制度与实践被历史地生产出来。)  
  
**Use when asking:**  
What makes this statement count as truth? What institution authorizes it? What body, norm, or subject does it produce?  
(什么使这个陈述算作真理？什么制度授权它？它生产什么身体、规范或主体？)  
  
**Typical sentence:** The diagnosis does not merely describe the patient; it places the person inside a medical regime of truth.  
(诊断并不只是描述病人；它把人放入医学真理体制之中。)  
  
**Misuse warning:** Foucauldian analysis should not reduce everything to vague “power.” It must specify the apparatus, technique, norm, institution, and subject-position.  
(福柯式分析不应把一切化约为模糊的“权力”。它必须指出装置、技术、规范、制度和主体位置。)  
  
### 8. If the Problem Is “What Desire or Symptom Structures It?”, Use Psychoanalytic Vocabulary  
  
Use this vocabulary when the issue concerns **unconscious**, **desire**, **lack**, **fantasy**, **symptom**, **repetition**, **jouissance**, or **split subjectivity**.  
  
Core vocabulary: **Unconscious (无意识; de: das Unbewusste; fr: inconscient)**, **Repression (压抑; de: Verdrängung; fr: refoulement)**, **Symptom (症状; fr: symptôme)**, **Drive (驱力; de: Trieb; fr: pulsion)**, **Repetition Compulsion (重复强迫; de: Wiederholungszwang)**, **Desire (欲望; fr: désir)**, **Lack (缺失; fr: manque)**, **Fantasy (幻想; fr: fantasme)**, **objet petit a (小客体 a; fr: objet petit a)**, **Jouissance (享乐; fr: jouissance)**, **Real (实在界; fr: le Réel)**.  
  
**Problem solved:** this vocabulary reveals unconscious structures that organize speech, action, attachment, and suffering.  
(这一词汇揭示组织言说、行动、依附和痛苦的无意识结构。)  
  
**Use when asking:**  
What does the subject repeat? What lack organizes desire? What fantasy stages the relation to the Other? Where does language fail?  
(主体重复什么？什么缺失组织欲望？什么幻想安排同大他者的关系？语言在哪里失败？)  
  
**Typical sentence:** The character says they want success, but the narrative shows attachment to a fantasy of failure.  
(角色声称想要成功，但叙事显示其依附于失败幻想。)  
  
**Misuse warning:** psychoanalysis should not be used as casual diagnosis of real people. Use it structurally: symptom, fantasy, repetition, desire, and speech-position.  
(精神分析不应用作对真实个人的随意诊断。应结构性使用：症状、幻想、重复、欲望和言说位置。)  
  
### 9. If the Problem Is “Whose Body or Labor Is Hidden?”, Use Feminist Vocabulary  
  
Use this vocabulary when the issue concerns **gender**, **body**, **care**, **reproductive labor**, **domestic labor**, **patriarchy**, **standpoint**, or **bodily autonomy**.  
  
Core vocabulary: **Feminism (女性主义; fr: féminisme)**, **Patriarchy (父权制; en: patriarchy)**, **Sex (生理性别; la: sexus)**, **Gender (社会性别; en: gender)**, **Embodiment (具身性; de: Leiblichkeit; en: embodiment)**, **Care (照护; fr: soin; en: care)**, **Social Reproduction (社会再生产; en: social reproduction)**, **Domestic Labor (家务劳动; en: domestic labor)**, **Emotional Labor (情绪劳动; en: emotional labor)**, **Bodily Autonomy (身体自主; en: bodily autonomy)**, **Intersectionality (交叉性; en: intersectionality)**.  
  
**Problem solved:** this vocabulary reveals how supposedly universal concepts depend on gendered bodies, hidden care, and unequal labor.  
(这一词汇揭示所谓普遍概念如何依赖性别化身体、隐藏照护和不平等劳动。)  
  
**Use when asking:**  
Whose labor sustains the scene? Whose body is regulated? Whose standpoint is dismissed? Which women or gendered subjects are being falsely universalized?  
(谁的劳动支撑这个场景？谁的身体被规制？谁的立场被驳回？哪些女性或性别化主体被错误普遍化？)  
  
**Typical sentence:** The theory praises autonomy while hiding the care labor that makes autonomy possible.  
(该理论赞美自主性，却隐藏了使自主性成为可能的照护劳动。)  
  
**Misuse warning:** feminism is not only about adding women. It asks how the universal was constructed through gendered exclusion.  
(女性主义不只是“加入女性”。它追问普遍者如何通过性别化排除被建构。)  
  
### 10. If the Problem Is “What Norm Produces Sexual or Gender Identity?”, Use Queer Vocabulary  
  
Use this vocabulary when the issue concerns **sexuality**, **gender identity**, **heteronormativity**, **performativity**, **compulsory heterosexuality**, **queerness**, or **normative recognition**.  
  
Core vocabulary: **Queer (酷儿; en: queer)**, **Performativity (表演性; en: performativity)**, **Heteronormativity (异性恋规范性; en: heteronormativity)**, **Compulsory Heterosexuality (强制性异性恋; en: compulsory heterosexuality)**, **Recognition (承认; de: Anerkennung; en: recognition)**, **Misrecognition (误认; en: misrecognition)**, **Gender Norm (性别规范; en: gender norm)**, **Anti-Normativity (反规范性; en: anti-normativity)**.  
  
**Problem solved:** this vocabulary reveals how gender and sexuality are produced as natural, normal, deviant, recognizable, or unintelligible.  
(这一词汇揭示性别与性如何被生产为自然的、正常的、异常的、可承认的或不可理解的。)  
  
**Use when asking:**  
What desire is normalized? What identity must be repeated to become recognizable? What form of life is made unintelligible?  
(什么欲望被规范化？什么身份必须被重复才变得可承认？什么生活形式被制造为不可理解？)  
  
**Typical sentence:** The romance plot appears natural because heterosexual completion has been built into the narrative form.  
(这个爱情情节显得自然，是因为异性恋完成被建入叙事形式。)  
  
**Misuse warning:** queer theory does not merely name LGBT content. It questions the authority of norms that make some identities recognizable and others deviant.  
(酷儿理论不只是命名 LGBT 内容。它质疑那些使某些身份可承认、另一些身份异常化的规范权威。)  
  
### 11. If the Problem Is “What Empire or Race Is Forgotten?”, Use Postcolonial Vocabulary  
  
Use this vocabulary when the issue concerns **empire**, **colonialism**, **race**, **Orientalism**, **subalternity**, **colonial knowledge**, **decolonization**, or **global hierarchy**.  
  
Core vocabulary: **Colonialism (殖民主义; la: colonia; en: colonialism)**, **Imperialism (帝国主义; la: imperium; en: imperialism)**, **Empire (帝国; la: imperium; en: empire)**, **Orientalism (东方主义; en: Orientalism)**, **Othering (他者化; en: othering)**, **Race (种族; en: race)**, **Racialization (种族化; en: racialization)**, **Subaltern (底层者; it: subalterno; en: subaltern)**, **Epistemic Violence (认识暴力; en: epistemic violence)**, **Hybridity (混杂性; en: hybridity)**, **Mimicry (拟态; en: mimicry)**, **Decolonization (去殖民化; fr: décolonisation; en: decolonization)**.  
  
**Problem solved:** this vocabulary reveals how modernity, knowledge, culture, and development are shaped by empire, race, extraction, and global inequality.  
(这一词汇揭示现代性、知识、文化和发展如何由帝国、种族、榨取和全球不平等塑造。)  
  
**Use when asking:**  
Who is represented as backward? Who speaks for whom? What archive produces the colonized as knowable? What global hierarchy is hidden?  
(谁被表象为落后？谁替谁说话？什么档案把被殖民者生产为可知对象？什么全球等级被隐藏？)  
  
**Typical sentence:** The development narrative appears universal only by forgetting the colonial extraction that made its standard possible.  
(发展叙事只有通过遗忘使其标准成为可能的殖民榨取，才显得普遍。)  
  
**Misuse warning:** postcolonial theory is not a generic anti-Western gesture. It is a precise analysis of empire, representation, race, archive, extraction, and knowledge.  
(后殖民理论不是泛泛的反西方姿态。它是对帝国、表象、种族、档案、榨取和知识的精确分析。)  
  
### 12. If the Problem Is “What Does It Do in Practice?”, Use Pragmatist Vocabulary  
  
Use this vocabulary when the issue concerns **practice**, **consequence**, **habit**, **inquiry**, **fallibilism**, **belief**, **problem-solving**, or **usefulness under disciplined inquiry**.  
  
Core vocabulary: **Pragmatism (实用主义; en: pragmatism)**, **Practice (实践; el: πρᾶξις; en: practice)**, **Consequence (后果; la: consequentia; en: consequence)**, **Inquiry (探究; en: inquiry)**, **Habit (习惯; la: habitus; en: habit)**, **Belief (信念; en: belief)**, **Doubt (怀疑; la: dubitatio; en: doubt)**, **Fallibilism (可错论; en: fallibilism)**, **Abduction (溯因; en: abduction)**, **Instrumentalism (工具主义; en: instrumentalism)**.  
  
**Problem solved:** this vocabulary reveals the practical difference a concept, belief, or theory makes.  
(这一词汇揭示一个概念、信念或理论造成什么实践差异。)  
  
**Use when asking:**  
What changes if this belief is accepted? What problem does this concept solve? What habits does it form? How can inquiry revise it?  
(如果接受这个信念，会改变什么？这个概念解决什么问题？它形成什么习惯？探究如何修正它？)  
  
**Typical sentence:** The concept is valuable only if it changes inquiry or action in a determinate way.  
(该概念只有在以确定方式改变探究或行动时才有价值。)  
  
**Misuse warning:** pragmatism is not crude usefulness. It requires disciplined inquiry, consequences, correction, and public testing.  
(实用主义不是粗浅的有用性。它要求有规训的探究、后果、修正和公共检验。)  
  
### 13. If the Problem Is “Is the Word Being Misused?”, Use Ordinary Language Vocabulary  
  
Use this vocabulary when the issue concerns **ordinary use**, **language-games**, **rule-following**, **speech acts**, **performative force**, or **category mistakes**.  
  
Core vocabulary: **Ordinary Language Philosophy (日常语言哲学; en: ordinary language philosophy)**, **Use (使用; de: Gebrauch)**, **Language-Game (语言游戏; de: Sprachspiel)**, **Form of Life (生活形式; de: Lebensform)**, **Rule-Following (遵循规则; de: Regelfolgen)**, **Family Resemblance (家族相似; de: Familienähnlichkeit)**, **Private Language (私人语言; de: Privatsprache)**, **Speech Act (言语行为; en: speech act)**, **Performative (施为性话语; en: performative)**, **Category Mistake (范畴错误; en: category mistake)**.  
  
**Problem solved:** this vocabulary reveals philosophical confusion caused by taking words outside their practical grammar.  
(这一词汇揭示由于把词语抽离其实践语法而造成的哲学混乱。)  
  
**Use when asking:**  
How is the word actually used? What action does the utterance perform? What language-game gives it sense? Is a category mistake occurring?  
(这个词实际上如何被使用？该话语执行什么行动？什么语言游戏赋予它意义？是否发生范畴错误？)  
  
**Typical sentence:** The problem disappears once “mind” is no longer treated as the name of a hidden inner object.  
(一旦不再把“心灵”当作隐藏内部对象的名称，这个问题就消失了。)  
  
**Misuse warning:** ordinary language philosophy does not worship common speech. It uses ordinary grammar to expose philosophical distortion.  
(日常语言哲学并不崇拜日常话语。它使用日常语法来暴露哲学扭曲。)  
  
### 14. If the Problem Is “What System Is Being Built by Technology?”, Use Contemporary Critical Vocabulary  
  
Use this vocabulary when the issue concerns **technology**, **data**, **platforms**, **algorithms**, **AI**, **automation**, **infrastructure**, **extraction**, or **planetary crisis**.  
  
Core vocabulary: **Technology (技术; de: Technik)**, **Technics (技术性; fr: technique)**, **Enframing (集置; de: Gestell)**, **Infrastructure (基础设施; en: infrastructure)**, **Data (数据; la: datum)**, **Datafication (数据化; en: datafication)**, **Algorithm (算法; en: algorithm)**, **Algorithmic Governance (算法治理; en: algorithmic governance)**, **Model (模型; en: model)**, **Prediction (预测; en: prediction)**, **Automation (自动化; en: automation)**, **Platform (平台; en: platform)**, **Surveillance Capitalism (监控资本主义; en: surveillance capitalism)**, **AI Agent (AI 智能体; en: AI agent)**, **Anthropocene (人类世; el: ἄνθρωπος + καινός; en: Anthropocene)**, **Extraction (榨取; la: extrahere; en: extraction)**.  
  
**Problem solved:** this vocabulary reveals how technical systems organize knowledge, labor, desire, governance, and environment.  
(这一词汇揭示技术系统如何组织知识、劳动、欲望、治理和环境。)  
  
**Use when asking:**  
What is represented as data? What model acts on it? What behavior is predicted? What institution acts on the output? What labor and extraction are hidden?  
(什么被表征为数据？什么模型作用于它？什么行为被预测？什么制度根据输出行动？什么劳动和榨取被隐藏？)  
  
**Typical sentence:** The platform appears as convenience, but it functions as infrastructure for data extraction and behavioral governance.  
(平台显得像便利工具，但它作为数据榨取和行为治理的基础设施运作。)  
  
**Misuse warning:** technology critique is not anti-technology. It rejects technological innocence, not technical invention itself.  
(技术批判不是反技术。它拒绝技术无辜论，而不是拒绝技术发明本身。)  
  
### 15. Fast Diagnostic Table  
  
**If the text asks “what is real?”** activate **Ontology (本体论; el: ὄν + λόγος)**.  
(如果文本追问“什么是真实的？”，调用本体论。)  
  
**If the text asks “how is this known?”** activate **Epistemology (认识论; el: ἐπιστήμη + λόγος)**.  
(如果文本追问“这是如何被认识的？”，调用认识论。)  
  
**If the text asks “who is speaking or acting?”** activate **Subjectivity (主体性; de: Subjektivität)**.  
(如果文本追问“谁在说话或行动？”，调用主体性理论。)  
  
**If the text asks “what does this mean?”** activate **Language, Sign, and Interpretation (语言、符号与解释)**.  
(如果文本追问“这意味着什么？”，调用语言、符号与解释。)  
  
**If the text asks “what structure organizes this?”** activate **Structuralism (结构主义; fr: structuralisme)**.  
(如果文本追问“什么结构组织了它？”，调用结构主义。)  
  
**If the text asks “what has been excluded?”** activate **Deconstruction (解构; fr: déconstruction)**.  
(如果文本追问“什么被排除了？”，调用解构。)  
  
**If the text asks “what truth-regime produced this?”** activate **Foucault (福柯式分析; fr: foucaldien)**.  
(如果文本追问“什么真理体制生产了它？”，调用福柯式分析。)  
  
**If the text asks “what unconscious desire returns here?”** activate **Psychoanalysis (精神分析; de: Psychoanalyse)**.  
(如果文本追问“什么无意识欲望在此返回？”，调用精神分析。)  
  
**If the text asks “whose body or labor is hidden?”** activate **Feminist Theory (女性主义理论; en: feminist theory)**.  
(如果文本追问“谁的身体或劳动被隐藏？”，调用女性主义理论。)  
  
**If the text asks “what norm makes this desire natural?”** activate **Queer Theory (酷儿理论; en: queer theory)**.  
(如果文本追问“什么规范使这种欲望显得自然？”，调用酷儿理论。)  
  
**If the text asks “what empire or race is forgotten?”** activate **Postcolonial Theory (后殖民理论; en: postcolonial theory)**.  
(如果文本追问“什么帝国或种族被遗忘？”，调用后殖民理论。)  
  
**If the text asks “what practical difference does this make?”** activate **Pragmatism (实用主义; en: pragmatism)**.  
(如果文本追问“这造成什么实践差异？”，调用实用主义。)  
  
**If the text asks “how is the word used?”** activate **Ordinary Language Philosophy (日常语言哲学; en: ordinary language philosophy)**.  
(如果文本追问“这个词如何被使用？”，调用日常语言哲学。)  
  
**If the text asks “what technical system is being built?”** activate **Contemporary Critical Technology Vocabulary (当代技术批判词汇)**.  
(如果文本追问“什么技术系统正在被建构？”，调用当代技术批判词汇。)  
  
### 16. Minimal Working Formula  
  
A complete philosophical reading can be built from one sentence pattern:  
  
**This concept appears to mean X, but historically it was formed to solve Y; it works by distinguishing A from B; it hides C; it produces D; and in the present context it should be used to diagnose E.**  
(这个概念表面上意味着 X，但在历史上它是为了解决 Y 而形成的；它通过区分 A 与 B 运作；它隐藏 C；它生产 D；在当前语境中，它应被用来诊断 E。)  
  
Example:  
  
**Gender (社会性别; en: gender)** appears to mean identity, but historically it was mobilized to separate social norm from biological determinism; it works by distinguishing sexed bodies from gendered expectations; it hides the institutional production of normality when treated as natural; it produces recognizable masculine and feminine subjects; and in the present context it should be used to diagnose how repeated norms make identity appear stable.  
(**Gender** 表面上意味着身份，但在历史上它被动员出来，是为了把社会规范同生物决定论区分开；它通过区分性化身体与性别化期待而运作；当它被自然化时，会隐藏正常性的制度生产；它生产可承认的男性化和女性化主体；在当前语境中，它应被用来诊断重复规范如何使身份显得稳定。)  
  
### 17. Final Quick Rule  
  
**A philosophical term is ready for use only when four things are clear:**  
(一个哲学术语只有在四件事清楚时才可以使用：)  
  
**Definition:** what it means.  
(定义：它意味着什么。)  
  
**Problem:** what it solves.  
(问题：它解决什么。)  
  
**Operation:** how it works.  
(操作：它如何运作。)  
  
**Risk:** what it may hide or distort.  
(风险：它可能隐藏或扭曲什么。)  
  
The strongest final question remains:  
  
**What problem is this vocabulary built to diagnose, and what becomes visible only after this vocabulary is used?**  
(这组词汇被建构出来是为了诊断什么问题？只有在使用这组词汇之后，什么才变得可见？)
